   vāsiṣṭhārthatvena nārāśaṃsamantravidhānamaṅgīkṛtam, tadvadihāpi	vAsizWa-arTa-tvena nArASaMsa-mantra-viDAnam-aFgIkRtam, tadvat-iha-api
   paraṃparāsaṃbandhena vṛṣṭyarthahīṣādiniyamavidhyupapatterna lakṣaṇāpīti	paraMparA-saMbanDena vRzwi-arTa-hIza-Adi-niyama-viDi-upapatteH-na lakzaNA-api-iti
   pakṣāntaramāha --------- vastutastviti //	pakza-antaram-Aha -------- vastutas-tu-iti //
   saubharaviśeṣa eveti //	sOBara-viSezaH eva-iti //
   hīṣādinidhanaghaṭitasaubharaviśeṣa evetyarthaḥ /	hIza-Adi-niDana-Gawita-sOBara-viSezaH eva-iti-arTaH /
   ataśceti //	atas-ca-iti //
   vṛṣṭau hīṣeva vijātīyasaubharadvārā kuryāditi niyamavidhyarthe phalite	vRzwO hIzA-iva vijAtIya-sOBara-dvArA kuryAt-iti niyama-viDi-arTe Palite
   vṛṣṭyarthasaubharavidhāvapi vṛṣṭyarthaṃ vijātīyānāṃ saubharāṇāṃ vikalpena	vRzwi-arTa-sOBara-viDO=-api vRzwi-arTam vijAtIyAnAm sOBarANAm vikalpena
   prāptānāṃ hīṣnidhanakasyaiva saubharaviśeṣasya vṛṣṭisādhanatā	prAptAnAm hi-izni-Danakasya-eva sOBara-viSezasya vRzwi-sADana-tA
   nānyeṣāmityapi niyamāntaraṃ phalitaṃ bhavati /	na-anyezAm-iti-api niyama-antaram Palitam Bavati /
   nahi bhinnanidhanakasaubharasya vṛṣṭyādyarthatvena tādṛśaniyamāntarābhāve	na-hi Binna-niDanaka-sOBarasya vRzwi-Adi-arTa-tvena tAdRSa-niyama-antara-aBAve
   vṛṣṭau hīṣeveti niyamaḥ kathamapi saṃpādayituṃ śakyate /	vRzwO hIzA-iva-iti niyamaH kaTam-api saMpAdayitum Sakyate /
   nidhanāntarayuktasyāpi saubharasya tadarthaṃ kriyamāṇatvāt //	niDana-antara-yuktasya-api sOBarasya tad-arTam kriyamANa-tvAt //
   (kāṃsyabhojinyāyasvarūpaṃ, tena prakṛtārthanirṇayaḥ,	(kAMsya-Boji-nyAya-sva-rUpaM, tena prakRta-arTa-nirNayaH,
   pūrvottarakalpaprayojanaṃ ca) ataśca yathaiva śiṣyācāryayoḥ saha	pUrva-uttara-kalpa-prayojanam ca) atas-ca yaTA-eva Sizya-AcAryayoH saha
   bhojanaprāptau śiṣyasya kāṃsyabhojitvaniyamamaniyatapātrabhojyā- cāryo	Bojana-prAptO Sizyasya kAMsya-Bojitva-niyamam-aniyata-pAtra-BojyA ca-AryaH-
   'nurundhāno loke dṛśyata iti dvādaśādhikaraṇe kāṃsyabhojinyāye vakṣyate,	anurunDAnaH loke dRSyate iti dvAdaSa-aDikaraNe kAMsya-Boji-nyAye vakzyate,
   tena nyāyena vṛṣṭyarthasaubharavidhiraniyatasaubharagrāhyopi	tena nyAyena vRzwi-arTa-sOBara-viDiH-aniyata-sOBara-grAhya-upi
   dvitīyaniyamamanurundhāno hīṣādinidhanaghaṭitasaubharaviśeṣameva gṛhṇātīti	dvitIya-niyamam-anurunDAnaH hi-iza-Adi-niDana-Gawita-sOBara-viSezam-eva gRhNAti-iti
   siddhaṃ niyamāntaramityarthaḥ /	sidDam niyama-antaram-iti-arTaH /
   kva tarhi śākhāntarasthasaubharasya niveśa ityapekṣāyāmāha ----------	kva tarhi SAKA-antara-sTa-sOBarasya niveSaH iti-apekzAyAm-Aha ----------
   ataśceti //	atas-ca-iti //
   siddhānte saubharaphalāt vṛṣṭyādernātiriktaṃ vṛṣṭyādiphalaṃ hīṣādibhya iti	sidDAnte sOBara-PalAt vRzwi-AdeH-na-atiriktam vRzwi-Adi-Palam hIza-AdiByaH iti
   prayojanaṃ vyatirekata eva jñātuṃ śakyamiti noktam //	prayojanam vyatirekataH eva jQAtum Sakyam-iti na-uktam //
   // iti trayodaśaṃ saubharādhikaraṇam //	// iti trayodaSam sOBara-aDikaraNam //
   iti kavimaṇḍana - khaṇḍadevaśiṣya - śaṃbhubhaṭṭaviracitāyāṃ	iti kavi-maNxana  KaNxa-deva-Sizya  SaMBu-Bawwa-viracitAyAm
   bhāṭṭadīpikāvyākhyāyāṃ prabhāvalyāṃ dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ //. //	BAwwa-dIpikA-vyAKyAyAm praBAvalyAm dvitIya-aDyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH //. //
